This is an exception, goes straight 
from pillar post to low-tier post ^h8jBykMH

1. Best of?
This question has many derivatives like: 
- Best for adults/young adults/teens (or really any demographic) 
- Best free
- Most spicey/steamy <insert any other adjective here>
- Best to read online
- Best on a certain platform
- Best featuring something (like a trope, character type, or theme)
- Best of specific time period or all time
- Best for reading when (insert topic, theme, time of year, activity)

2. Most of?
- Most famous/popular
- Most bought
- most/highest ranked
- most explicit/spicy/steamy/fun/innocent
- most attractive/interesting characters in books within genre


3. Who is/are? + any of the other question categories
- who is the number 1/best of a genre
- who are the best/newest/
- who are the readers of
- New York Times best selling
- who writes within this category/genre/trope


5. Miscellaneous questions
- What are the elements of?
- What is the heat level?
- What defines/constitutes/is considered a genre/trope/category/character type
